<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of 2014 Winter Olympics medal winners</h1>			<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
				<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>				<div id="contentSub"></div>

<p>The <b><a href="/wiki/2014_Winter_Olympics" title="2014 Winter Olympics">2014 Winter Olympics</a></b>, officially the <b>XXII Olympic Winter Games</b>, or the 22nd <a href="/wiki/Winter_Olympic_Games" title="Winter Olympic Games">Winter Olympics</a>, took place from 7 to 23 February 2014, in <a href="/wiki/Sochi" title="Sochi">Sochi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> 98 events in 15 winter sport disciplines were held, with gold, silver and bronze medals were awarded in each event. These Games were affected by the <a href="/wiki/Doping_in_Russia" title="Doping in Russia">Russian doping scandal</a> with 4 of Russia's original 33 medals stripped for alleged doping violations.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Alpine_skiing">Alpine skiing</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2014_Winter_Olympics_medal_winners&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Alpine skiing">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Alpine_skiing_at_the_2014_Winter_Olympics" title="Alpine skiing at the 2014 Winter Olympics">Alpine skiing at the 2014 Winter Olympics</a></div>
<h3><span id="Men.27s_events"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Men's_events">Men's events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2014_Winter_Olympics_medal_winners&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Men's events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg/220px-Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg" width="220" height="199" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg/330px-Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a6/Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg/440px-Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1355" data-file-height="1227"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Men%27sDownhillSochi2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The medalists in men's downhill</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg/220px-SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg" width="220" height="145" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg/330px-SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg/440px-SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4320" data-file-height="2846"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:SuperCombinedMSochi2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The medalists in men's super combined</div></div></div>
<p>Two bronze medals, one to Canada and one to United States, were awarded for a third-place tie in the <a href="/wiki/Alpine_skiing_at_the_2014_Winter_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_super-G" title="Alpine skiing at the 2014 Winter Olympics  Men's super-G">men's super-G event</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span id="Women.27s_events"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_events">Women's events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2014_Winter_Olympics_medal_winners&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Women's events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Women%27s_downhill,_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg/220px-Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg" width="220" height="217" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg/330px-Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg/440px-Women%27s_downhill%2C_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1072" data-file-height="1056"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Women%27s_downhill,_2014_WOG_cropped.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The medalists in women's downhill</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg/220px-LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg" width="220" height="286" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg/330px-LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg/440px-LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1607" data-file-height="2088"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:LadiesSuperCombinedSochi2014.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The medalists in ladies' super combined</div></div></div>
<p>Two gold medals, one to Slovenia and one to Switzerland, were awarded for a first-place tie in the <a href="/wiki/Alpine_skiing_at_the_2014_Winter_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_downhill" title="Alpine skiing at the 2014 Winter Olympics  Women's downhill">women's downhill event</a>. No silver medal was awarded.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span id="Women.27s_events_7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_events_7">Women's events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_2014_Winter_Olympics_medal_winners&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Women's events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg/220px-Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg" width="220" height="330" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg/330px-Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg/440px-Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1824" data-file-height="2737"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Korea_Lee_Sanghwa_500m_04.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The medalists in 500 m ladies' speed skating.  Silver medalist <a href="/wiki/Olga_Fatkulina" title="Olga Fatkulina">Olga Fatkulina</a> of Russia was subsequently stripped of the silver medal on 24 November 2017 by IOC, but <a href="/wiki/Court_of_Arbitration_for_Sport" title="Court of Arbitration for Sport">CAS</a>  returned the medal to her on 1 Feb 2018.</div></div></div>
